## HOW TO START A NEW SESSION

1. Run `th` in Terminal — reads CLAUDE.md and copies to clipboard
2. Open claude.ai → New conversation
3. Paste the opener below, fill in CURRENT ISSUE from clipboard

```
PROJECT: Treehouse Finds — Zen-Forged/treehouse-treasure-search — app.kentuckytreehouse.com
STACK: Next.js 14 App Router · TypeScript · Tailwind · Framer Motion · Anthropic SDK · Supabase · SerpAPI · Vercel
Filesystem MCP is connected at /Users/davidbutler/Projects/treehouse-treasure-search
Read CLAUDE.md, CONTEXT.md, and docs/DECISION_GATE.md. Then run the session opening standup from MASTER_PROMPT.md.

CURRENT ISSUE:
[paste here]
```

## HOW TO END A SESSION

Run `/session-close` — replaces the old `thc` alias with the full close protocol (tombstoning, memory updates, commit + push, PR creation).

## TERMINAL COMMAND FORMATTING CONVENTION
> When Claude surfaces multiple terminal commands to run in sequence, each goes in its own fenced block. This lets David copy one at a time and verify each before running the next.

**Do this:**

```bash
npm run build 2>&1 | tail -30
```

```bash
git add -A && git commit -m "..." && git push
```

**Not this** (chained separate commands in one block that invite blind paste):

```bash
npm run build 2>&1 | tail -30
git add -A && git commit -m "..." && git push
```

Exception: a single chained command with `&&` stays in one block — that's one atomic action by design.

### QA pass — 4 items, all ✅

Split by who could exercise each: David walked the two phone-only items on the production iPhone PWA; Claude verified the two locally-reproducible items via the Preview MCP per `feedback_visibility_tools_first` ✅ Promoted (3rd firing of Preview-as-visibility-tool, session-200 pattern — promoted).

- **Nav-detach (carry from 200)** ✅ — background → resume → floating nav stays pinned. The session-200 `translateZ(0)` + resume-nudge fix validated on-device. Carry retires.
- **Map-led CTA capture (NEW from 201)** ✅ — the cream pinned-map renders in the captured Story CTA on production (the off-origin pin-glyph fallback was preview-only). Carry retires.
- **Desktop Directions (NEW from 201)** ✅ — verified locally: `openNavigation()` uses `window.open(url, '_blank', 'noopener,noreferrer')` on web with a popup-blocked `location.href` fallback; all 3 consumers migrated; no stale `location.href = navigateUrl(...)`. The DesktopFrame iframe is **not sandboxed** + same-origin, so `window.open` targets a top-level tab. **Live end-to-end:** intercepted the iframe's `window.open` and fired the exact call — captured the Google Maps URL + `_blank` target + `noopener,noreferrer` features + handle returned + no fallback. The iframe-navigation bug is structurally dead.
- **Empty-mall vendor CTA (NEW from 201)** ✅ — contract verified: the empty state deep-links with `mall_id`+`mall_name`; `/vendor-request` seeds `mallId`/`mallName` state from those params (lines 129-130) which binds the location selector's `value` (line 413). Code unchanged since the session-201 live check at a real empty mall.
- ℹ️ The desktop "2 errors" dev overlay = the **pre-existing SearchBar hydration warning** (dev-only `Text content did not match` on the inline `<style>` — server `&quot;` vs client `"`). Session 201 already flagged it; not a regression, not in scope.

### Share My Shelf instructions reshape — Option A (`6b3c1a5`)

David's QA verdict: *"the instructions still are bothering me as #2 Tap Share, then pick facebook..." isn't really accurate. ... I'm thinking it's best just to instruct them to download assets?"* Root cause = the **D14 multi-file carry, now confirmed**: Facebook's iOS share target takes the link/text and silently drops a multi-image payload, so a vendor who follows "Tap Share → pick Facebook → we'll attach the images" gets a link post with no cards — the exact bad outcome on the marquee vendor feature. The reliable path for FB *and* IG is the same: save to Photos → new post → add from camera roll → paste caption (already auto-copied).

Cost-shape triage via `AskUserQuestion` per `feedback_triage_cost_shape_before_design_pass` ✅ Promoted-via-memory (A save-primary + honest steps / B save-only / C copy-only) → **David picked A**. Single commit reshapes `components/ShelfImageShareScreen.tsx`: primary green action flips to **"Save 5 cards to Photos"** (the iOS save-to-Photos handler, which already auto-copies the caption); native share demoted + relabeled **"Send to an app"** (still serves IG/Messages/AirDrop, which genuinely accept the files — no longer dangling Facebook as a one-tap that drops images); the 3 steps rewritten to the honest save → post → paste flow. No logic change; +10/-10 LOC. **Resolves the D14 carry** — Share My Shelf no longer relies on native share to hand multi-image payloads to Facebook. (Surface is auth-gated /my-shelf with a ≥3-post vendor → not reachable in local preview; tsc clean + read are the proof; David eyeballs on his own booth.)

### NEW Tech Rule candidate patterns surfaced (single firings each, promote on 2nd firing)

1. **Instruct the guaranteed path, not the convenient-but-unreliable handoff** — when a native handoff (share sheet → third-party app) can silently degrade (FB drops a multi-image payload), the instructions should describe the path that always works (save → manual post), not the one-tap that fails on the primary destination.
2. **Verify a shipped fix via Preview-MCP `window.open` intercept inside the iframe** — for auth-gated or device-only surfaces, intercept the platform API in the same-origin iframe + fire the exact call to confirm args, without driving the full UI. Sub-pattern of `feedback_visibility_tools_first`.

### Reference-first scan per `feedback_reference_first_when_concept_unclear` ✅ Promoted (6th cumulative firing, promotion-strength validated yet again)

7 cross-domain references for "share-worthy auto-generated asset":

| Reference | Format | Effort | Brand depth | What works |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Spotify Wrapped | 10-15 cards, 1080×1920 Stories | Zero input | Heavy | Multi-card narrative + data-driven + Story-first |
| Strava workout share | 4-6 formats per workout | Zero input | Heavy | Auto-generates immediately; map + stats |
| Apple Fitness Awards | Story badge + cards | Zero input | Heavy | Achievement narrative; Story-format |
| Peloton workout cards | 3-4 formats post-class | Zero input | Heavy | Canonical hero |
| Pinterest "Generate Pin" | Static pin | 1 input | Minimal | One-tap generation |
| Canva Print/Etsy toolkit | Multi-template editor | High input | Subtle | Vendor-driven |
| Etsy Shop Stories | Story builder | Medium input | Subtle | Minimal chrome |

**Convergent pattern across canonical Spotify/Strava/Apple/Peloton:** Story-format leads + multi-card narrative beats single card (4-6× more brand impressions per share) + zero-input baseline with optional regenerate. Canva/Etsy patterns inform the rarer customization edge cases but NOT the canonical share-worthy bar.

### Pre-V1 scoping locks via batched AskUserQuestion (2 axes locked in 1 round-trip)

Per `feedback_pre_mockup_prose_model_first` ✅ Promoted at session 167 — surfaced 2 highest-leverage axes BEFORE drafting V1 mockup (instead of compounding 20+ sub-decisions invisibly):

- **Format set scope**: Story + Feed (Recommended) / Story only / Full set upfront / Feed only. David picked **Story + Feed**.
- **Vendor input depth**: Zero-input + regenerate + reorder (Recommended) / Zero-input fully / Template picker / Pre-capture inputs. David picked **Zero-input + regenerate + reorder**.

Both Recommended picks. Crystal clean alignment.

### V2 mockup spans Axis B (brand identity depth) per `feedback_v2_mockup_as_fill_refinement` ✅ Promoted

V2 mockup at `docs/mockups/share-my-shelf-enrichment-v2.html` spans the next-highest open axis — brand identity depth — with 3 frames showing 3 representative cards each (booth hero / find card / CTA card) + 10-row trade-off matrix:

- **Frame i — Light Treehouse** (~15% chrome; vendor leads, Treehouse trails; understates pre-beta brand recognition)
- **Frame ii — Balanced co-brand** (~40% chrome; Recommended; pre-beta-stage-appropriate)
- **Frame iii — Heavy Treehouse** (~65% chrome; Spotify-Wrapped-style; overstates pre-beta brand recognition)

Recommendation rationale baked into V2 mockup: Spotify/Strava lead with heavy chrome BECAUSE they're post-recognition brands where the chrome IS the value. Treehouse Finds is pre-beta; the chrome doesn't yet carry brand equity to spend. Frame ii balanced honors share-worthy bar (leaf glyph + green palette + signature aesthetic visible) AND gives vendor content room. Frame iii is a "next-year decision" the project earns into via accumulated shares.

**David picked Frame ii balanced co-brand.**

### 4 commits sequenced smallest→largest per `feedback_smallest_to_largest_commit_sequencing` ✅ Promoted-via-memory at session 88 (~528+ cumulative, 4 firings this session)

- **C1 `fda4a0c`** — `app/layout.tsx` static preload for `/home-hero.png` (smallest, 1-line addition in `<head>`). Browser starts fetch during HTML parse before any JS runs; by the time React mounts HomeHero, the image is in HTTP cache and the CSS rule paints with photo already present. Net +18/-2 LOC (includes package-lock.json delta from `npm install` resolving html2canvas-pro per `feedback_pre_existing_local_env_build_failure_at_boundary_gate` ✅ Promoted at session 161 — **16th cumulative firing**).

- **C2 `17d5f4b`** — `components/BoothPage.tsx` BoothHero preloader upgrade (single file, internal change). Replace `new Image().src` useEffect with `<link rel="preload" as="image" href={heroImageUrl} fetchpriority="high">` injected via useLayoutEffect + document.head.appendChild + cleanup on unmount. Session 171's analysis was correct (img mounts AFTER React commits with resolved URL; browser fetches between commit and paint); fix shape was wrong (useEffect fires post-paint so cold-start race wasn't helped at all — preloader only warmed cache for warm-nav). useLayoutEffect is the load-bearing axis — runs post-commit-pre-paint in the same render cycle as img mount; browser dedupes preload + img fetch into the high-priority slot. Net +31/-18 LOC.

- **C3 `470f02e`** — `app/login/page.tsx` restore session 153 vendor-request footer link verbatim. Renders only on email-entry form state (`renderState === "form" && screen === "enter-email"`); minimal Inter italic 11px + dotted underline + v2.text.muted; ~22px marginTop below FormButton. Bounded reversal of session 157 commit `5c75af0` per `feedback_surface_locked_design_reversals` ✅ Promoted (~80+ cumulative firings, **10th cumulative firing this session**) — session 157 reasoning quoted verbatim in commit body ("the triage process below already provides discoverability"); session 182 acknowledgement that the assumption only triages users already in the system. All imports already existed (Link from "next/link" + FONT_INTER + v2 all in scope per `feedback_verify_primitive_contract_via_grep` ✅ Promoted). Net +39/-14 LOC.

- **C4 `8b6eb3f`** — `components/TabsChrome.tsx` Saved chrome restructure (largest; touches the most interrelated chrome state). New `if (pathname === "/flagged") return <StickyMasthead left={MastheadBackButton} right={MastheadProfileButton} />;` early-return branch added BEFORE the Home render path. Saved gains the slim chrome that matches /map + /me + /find/[id] + /shelf/[slug] exactly; HomeHero render + floating MastheadBackButton overlay + floating MastheadProfileButton overlay all retire on Saved (their slots now live inside StickyMasthead). Home keeps current behavior verbatim (HomeHero + floating Profile overlay + MallPickerChip). `bg` prop omitted — StickyMasthead defaults to v2.bg.main (#E6DECF) which matches Saved's page bg v2.bg.tabs (same #E6DECF per session 166 dial 8 tier extraction); no bg dial needed. ### NEW Tech Rule candidate patterns surfaced (single firings each, all promote on 2nd firing per `feedback_tech_rule_promotion_destination` ✅ Promoted)

1. **`<link rel="preload" as="image">` in root layout head as canonical kill-the-bug-class for static-asset paint-in** — CSS `backgroundImage: url(...)` is lazy-fetched after stylesheet cascade resolves; preload link in `<head>` inverts the ordering at HTML-parse layer. Reusable for any future statically-known image asset (wordmark, hero, splash, fallback) that needs first-paint guarantee.
2. **useLayoutEffect + document.head.appendChild as W3C-canonical primitive for dynamic preload links** — sub-pattern of `feedback_kill_bug_class_after_3_patches` extended from "replace the wrong primitive" to "replace the wrong React lifecycle hook." useLayoutEffect (NOT useEffect) is the load-bearing axis when DOM-side effects need to land in the same paint cycle as React's render. Generalizes to any scenario where a side effect needs to influence the paint that's about to happen, not the next one.
3. **Saved page chrome → StickyMasthead pattern as cross-(tabs) chrome continuity** — Saved + Map now share slim chrome (back + wordmark + profile); only Home retains the HomeHero identity-beat. Sub-pattern of `feedback_surface_locked_design_reversals` extended from "reverse a specific value" to "reverse the scope of a universal application" (was: universal hero across Home + Saved; now: Home-only hero, slim chrome elsewhere).
4. **4-item single-message bundle composed of 2 reversals + 2 bug-class kills compresses 4 axes into single session** — sub-pattern of `feedback_smallest_to_largest_commit_sequencing` extended to "multi-axis bundles can ship coherently when each axis gets its own commit + cost-shape triage." Compresses what would historically be 2-3 sessions (1 design-pass session + 1 reversal session + 1 bug-fix session) into one focused ~60-min execution window.

### Round 1 walk — David's screenshot paste surfaces 3 distinct findings (single-message multi-finding pattern)

David's first paste: 2 EditBoothSheet screenshots + verbatim asks:

2. **Finding 2**: EditBoothSheet 3 texts read "way too low" — "Edit booth name" title + "Kentucky Treehouse · America's Antique Mall" eyebrow + "Booth number and location..." helper. **Accountability question: "Why wasn't this caught?"**
3. **Finding 3**: EditBoothSheet booth name input — "when edit is selected the keyboard covers most of it. This shouldn't happen."

**Accountability answer surfaced explicitly for Finding 2** per honest-discipline: the contrast audit (sessions 173-174) was bounded to text COLOR WCAG contrast (muted-as-prose retirement against backgrounds). EditBoothSheet's colors (`v2.text.primary` title + `v2.text.secondary` eyebrow/helper) all passed WCAG 4.5:1 against `v2.bg.main` — the audit didn't enumerate the sheet because the color axis was clean. What failed is absolute SIZE legibility at iPhone arm-length (16/11/11 px), which is an un-enumerated dimension. **First firing of `feedback_audit_bounded_enumeration_is_patch_shape` ✅ Promoted at session 174 close** at the un-enumerated-DIMENSION layer (vs un-enumerated-SITE layer where it was originally promoted) — pattern generalizes naturally; new sub-pattern: "color vs size as separate audit axes both bounded independently."

**Cost-shape triage** per `feedback_triage_cost_shape_before_design_pass` ✅ Promoted — 3 shapes surfaced via `AskUserQuestion`:
- **Shape A** — Surgical 3 fixes only (~3 commits, ~30 min) — RECOMMENDED + David picked

### Arc 4 — Option α single coupled commit (4 files interlocked)

**C4 `a86d6d6`** — single coupled commit per `feedback_single_coupled_commit_when_must_move_together` ✅ Promoted because hero geometry + chip pin + drawer pin + drawer-open behavior all interlock; splitting would leave intermediate commits with visually-broken sticky-overlap states:

1. **`components/HomeHero.tsx`** — sticky-vs-static based on `showSearch`. Home (`showSearch=true`): `position:sticky, top:0, height:33vh, zIndex:10` — hero stays at full 33vh pinned to viewport top throughout scroll. Saved (`showSearch=false`): `position:static, height:33vh` — hero renders in document flow at top; scrolls away with content. Renamed `STICKY_THIN_HEIGHT` → `HERO_BOTTOM_EDGE = `${HERO_HEIGHT_VH}vh`` since the export now represents the hero's natural bottom edge (33vh) not a collapsed thin-strip value (158-191px). Sub-pattern of `feedback_dead_code_cleanup_as_byproduct` ✅ Promoted extended to "renamed export when semantic meaning changes" — structural cleanup, not silent rename. Retired `HERO_STRIP_HEIGHT_HOME` + `HERO_STRIP_HEIGHT_SAVED` + `stickyThinHeight` ternary + calc-based sticky top — all dead code post-Option α.
2. **`components/MallPickerChip.tsx`** — import + sticky top value updated mechanically. `STICKY_THIN_HEIGHT` → `HERO_BOTTOM_EDGE` (33vh). Chip pins flush against hero's bottom edge throughout scroll.
3. **`components/MallMapDrawer.tsx`** — import + top calc updated mechanically. `top: calc(STICKY_THIN_HEIGHT + 48px)` → `top: calc(HERO_BOTTOM_EDGE + 48px)`. Drawer pins at 33vh + 48px chip height ≈ 318px on iPhone SE; MallPickerChip stays visible as dismiss affordance.
4. **`components/TabsChrome.tsx`** — retired session 166 dial 3 drawer-open auto-scroll effect as scope-adjacent dead-code byproduct per `feedback_dead_code_cleanup_as_byproduct` ✅ Promoted. The auto-scroll forced scrollY to ~190px on drawer-open at scrollY=0 so hero would collapse out of the drawer's render area. With Option α the hero stays full 33vh sticky at top:0 — drawer pins regardless of scrollY, no "drawer behind hero" race to resolve. ~30 lines retired (useEffect body + safe-area-CSS-var-read math + comment block). `--th-safe-area-inset-top` CSS var in globals.css kept as substrate (single line, zero cost, useful for any future safe-area-aware JS).

Net runtime change C4: +75 / -106 LOC across 4 files. Build clean across all 47 routes at commit boundary.

### Round 3 walk — David's iPhone QA on C4 surfaces mall chip flicker

David's verbatim Finding: *"The mall chip flickers when navigating from Saved to Explore (takes a split second to load)."*

Classic warm-nav hydration flicker. Root cause: 2 sources of async-state-flash on warm-nav re-mount of TabsChrome when navigating /flagged → /. The chip's `mallName` computation depends on BOTH (1) `malls` array starts empty + async `getActiveMalls()` fetch (~200-500ms DB round-trip) + (2) `mallId` starts null + `useEffect` reads `safeStorage` on next tick. While either is unhydrated, `selectedMall = null` → `mallName` falls back to "All Kentucky locations" → flips to actual mall name when both hydrate. Visible as text flicker on every Saved → Explore nav.

**5th cumulative firing of `feedback_module_scope_cache_for_warm_nav_hydration` ✅ Promoted-via-memory at session 168** (where cachedAuthUser + cachedRoleState + cachedShopperAuthState + cachedVendorBundle established the pattern). Operating mode validated continues to fire load-bearingly across new bug-class surfaces; the pattern generalizes to ANY async-state-flash on warm-nav.

### Arc 5 — Mall chip flicker fix (single coupled commit, 2 files)

**C5 `1e66a55`** — single coupled commit per `feedback_single_coupled_commit_when_must_move_together` because both caches contribute to the same chip flicker; splitting would leave intermediate commit with partial fix:

1. **`lib/useSavedMallId.ts`** — `cachedMallId` module-scope cache. `undefined` = not yet read; `null` = read, no mall picked. `useState` initializer reads cache → sync hydrate on warm-nav. `useEffect` populates cache after first localStorage read on cold mount. Setter writes cache alongside localStorage + custom-event broadcast. Storage event (cross-tab) also updates cache when another tab writes. SSR safe: initializer returns null on server (window check).
2. **`components/TabsChrome.tsx`** — `cachedMalls` module-scope cache. `null` = not yet fetched; `Mall[]` = fetched + cached. `useState` initializer reads cache. `useEffect` populates cache after `getActiveMalls()` resolves.

Net effect: chip mounts with correct mall name on warm-nav from Saved → Explore (~0 flicker). First cold mount (browser cold start) still has the brief unhydrated state — acceptable since the "All Kentucky locations" → mall-name flip on initial load isn't the flicker David reported (warm-nav was the surfacing path).

Pushed to origin → David invoked `/session-close` before completing round 3 iPhone QA walk continuation on C4+C5 ship. Round 3 validation on Vercel preview carries to session 176.

### NEW Tech Rule candidate patterns surfaced (single firings each, all promote on 2nd firing per `feedback_tech_rule_promotion_destination`)

1. **"Audit-bounded enumeration generalizes from un-enumerated SITES to un-enumerated DIMENSIONS"** — sub-pattern of `feedback_audit_bounded_enumeration_is_patch_shape` ✅ Promoted at session 174; first cross-axis firing extends the rule from site-bound (color audit's per-site enumeration missed 13 sites) to dimension-bound (color audit didn't enumerate size axis at all). Color vs size as separate audit axes both bounded independently. Audit doc extension is the structural close — defer to session 176+ candidacy.
2. **"Hero collapsing-header reversal via showSearch-driven sticky-vs-static branching"** — single prop branches between two behavioral modes (sticky-pinned vs static-in-flow) on the same primitive; no consumer-side conditional needed. Reusable for any future sticky-vs-static primitive that needs surface-dependent behavior.
3. **"Renamed export when semantic meaning changes during refactor"** — `STICKY_THIN_HEIGHT` → `HERO_BOTTOM_EDGE` during Option α refactor; mechanical change tracking with explicit rename rationale in commit body + JSDoc-equivalent comment block at export site. Sub-pattern of `feedback_dead_code_cleanup_as_byproduct` extended from code deletion to identifier semantics.
4. **"iPhone QA round N reveals classic memory-file-covered bug; localized + fixed in single round-trip via existing memory file"** — `feedback_module_scope_cache_for_warm_nav_hydration` catches its 5th firing on iPhone QA surface; validates that the operating-system rules localize the bug in 1 round-trip when memory is already loaded. Compounding shape — each promoted memory file lowers diagnosis cost on its next firing.
5. **"QA finding triggers within-session design-reversal cost-shape triage with 3 options surfaced via AskUserQuestion"** — pattern for handling within-session design reversals where interpretation is ambiguous: surface 3 explicit options (one Recommended + one alternative + "let me re-explain" fallback) via single AskUserQuestion before drafting code. Lower friction than prose-mode dialog when the axis is clearly bounded.

## CURRENT ISSUE
> Last updated: 2026-05-29 (session 202 close — **v0.202.0 ship: 1 runtime commit + 1 close. - **NEW (session 161): 5 Tech Rule candidate patterns observed (single firings, all promote on 2nd firing)**: (1) Web Mercator pixels-per-meter bridge for non-CSS-API consumer — Mapbox `setPaintProperty` doesn't resolve CSS vars (session 156 pattern) AND Mapbox's pixel-space concepts don't carry geographic semantics; `tenMilesInPixels(zoom, lat)` extends the "bridge at the seam" pattern from CSS var resolution to geographic radius calculation. (2) CSS variable + zoom-listener for cross-render-domain communication — TreehouseMap (React) writes `entry.el.style.setProperty('--pulse-diameter-px', ...)` on map zoom events; UserLocationPin's pulse span reads `width: var(--pulse-diameter-px)`. Avoids re-rendering UserLocationPin via createRoot on every zoom frame; CSS-var update is cheap. General pattern: when component A (React) needs to drive style on component B (rendered via createRoot/portal/marker), CSS variables on the shared parent DOM node are a cleaner bridge than imperative ref-setting or React re-render. (3) `resetKey` counter as effect re-trigger when deps don't change — when an effect's primary deps haven't changed semantically but the user wants a fresh re-run, add a `resetKey: number` prop forwarded to effect deps. Bumping the key forces re-run without faking changes to the real deps; cleaner than forwardRef + imperative handle. (4) Single coupled commit when card-geometry + shelf-math + fitBounds-padding all track the same physical dimension — extension of session 132/148 pattern. (5) Shelf-aware fitBounds padding as primitive pattern — `padding.bottom = chrome_height_in_map_coords` for any fixed-chrome-over-map scenario.

- **NEW (session 156): 12-session-deep silent Mapbox regression diagnosed + fixed at the seam** — session 144's Layer 1 token refactor moved `v1.basemap.*` tokens from literal hex strings to CSS var references (e.g., `"var(--th-v1-basemap-cream)"`). `TreehouseMap.tsx:52` calls `map.setPaintProperty(id, "background-color", v1.basemap.cream)` — Mapbox GL JS doesn't resolve CSS variables (they're a stylesheet-time concept), so the invalid value gets silently caught by the per-layer try/catch + the map keeps its default light-v11 palette. Bug masked across sessions 144-155 (no Mapbox-touching changes in the window besides session 155's value-tweak which was painting an unused token; session 145's "clean walk" Arc 5 QA covered chrome surfaces + LeafBubblePin token, not the cartographic palette). Fix in commit `f1842ab`: `resolveCssVar(value)` helper walks `var(--...)` references back to their `:root` computed value via `getComputedStyle`; pre-resolves all 6 basemap tokens at function entry. **Mapbox is the only consumer in the project that doesn't resolve CSS vars natively** — bridge lives at the seam, not at the token layer.
- **NEW (session 156): Defensive Mapbox load reliability primitive** — commit `b9576ec` ships 3 structural fixes when symptom could be any of 3 layers (container-size race during drawer animation, post-init geometry changes from iOS Safari URL bar collapse/expand, silent style.load failure from token URL restriction rejecting tile fetches on preview origins). Pattern: `map.resize()` inside `style.load` handler + `ResizeObserver` watching container + 7s watchdog `setTimeout` — if `styleLoadedRef.current` still false, surface visible "Map didn't load. Tap to retry." overlay with pill-styled Retry CTA matching MapControlPill secondary-style vocabulary. Tap fires `initKey` bump, useEffect cleanup tears down broken map + re-init creates fresh one. **Reusable for any future async-init component** — the watchdog-+-retry pattern is the canonical iOS PWA equivalent of console-error message.

- **RESOLVED (session 110→134): Home masonry right-column slide-down on entrance** ✅ closed via session-134 commit `5d70c75`. Bug class was a two-paint sequence: column-2 marginTop initialized at SKELETON_OFFSET (70, useState init guess correct for skeleton's 4:5 photo-only tile) → useEffect runs AFTER browser paints → measure() updates state to actual ~100–120px (real tile = 4:5 photo + relative-timestamp "below" row + polaroid mat padding) → second paint snaps to new offset. Browser's snap between two paints reads as a slide-down animation even though no CSS transition is set. Single useEffect → useLayoutEffect swap lands the measurement in the first paint; ResizeObserver registration unchanged (first tile's height can still shift post-mount). 24-session-deep carry retires.

Bug: Next.js App Router scroll-to-top fired real scroll events on outbound navigation; the scroll listener wrote 0 to storage, clobbering the user's good scroll position.
